***поражать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поражать.html>поража́ть</a> (4813)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поразить.html>порази́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">porazítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поражать.html>поража́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poražátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поразить.html>порази́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hit, to affect, to strike, to defeat <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to infect or harm</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вирус.html>ви́рус</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гепатит.html>гепати́та</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поражать.html>поража́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:клетка.html>кле́тки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:печень.html>пе́чени</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vírus gepatíta <b>poražájet</b> klétki péčeni.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Hepatitis virus <b>affects</b> (i.e. infects) the liver cells.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>они́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:продолжать.html>продолжа́ли</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поражать.html>поража́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:противник.html>проти́вника</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:штык.html>штыка́ми</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oní prodolžáli <b>poražátʹ</b> protívnika štykámi.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">They continued to <b>hit</b> the enemy with bayonets.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to amaze, to strike, to stagger, to startle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:поражать.html>поража́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:красота.html>красота́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разнообразие.html>разнообра́зие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>на́ших</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жи́зней</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Poražájet</b> krasotá i raznoobrázije nášix žíznej.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The beauty and diversity of our lives <b>is amazing</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***поразивший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поразить.html>порази́вший</a> (1883)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поразить.html>порази́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">porazívšij</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поразить.html>порази́ть</a> (1883)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разить.html>рази́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поразить.html>порази́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">porazítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поражать.html>поража́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hit, to affect, to strike, to defeat <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to infect or harm</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вирус.html>ви́рус</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поразить.html>порази́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:клетка.html>кле́тки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:печень.html>пе́чени</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vírus <b>porazíl</b> klétki péčeni.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The virus <b>has affected</b>  (i.e. infected) the liver cells.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:поразить.html>порази́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:противник.html>проти́вника</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>porazítʹ</b> protívnika</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to defeat the enemy</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to amaze, to strike, to stagger, to startle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:если.html>е́сли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вас</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:поразить.html>порази́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:красота.html>красото́й</a> кака́я-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:женщина.html>же́нщина</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жете</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вспомнить.html>вспо́мнить</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>была́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:одетый.html>оде́та</a>, - <a href = vnd.unilang:значить.html>зна́чит</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>была́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:одетый.html>оде́та</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:идеальный.html>идеа́льно</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jésli vas <b>porazíla</b> krasotój kakája-libo žénščina, no vy ne móžete vspómnitʹ, vo što oná bylá odéta, - znáčit, oná bylá odéta ideálʹno.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">If you <b>are struck</b> by the beauty of a woman but you cannot remember what she was wearing, it means she was dressed perfectly.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поразиться.html>порази́ться</a> (8170)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поразить.html>порази́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">porazítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>to be surprised/astonished/thunderstruck <i>(by)</i></li>

***порвать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:порвать.html>порва́ть</a> (5752)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рвать.html>рвать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порвать.html>порва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">porvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рвать.html>рвать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tear (rend)</li>
<li>to tear apart
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неисправный.html>неиспра́вный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:принтер.html>при́нтер</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порвать.html>порва́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бумага.html>бума́гу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ничто.html>ничего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:печатать.html>печа́тал</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Neisprávnyj príntɛr tólʹko <b>porvál</b> bumágu i ničevó ne pečátal.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The broken printer only <b>tore</b> the paper <b>apart</b> and didn't print anything.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to tear out</li>
<li>to break off (a relationship)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рвать.html>рвать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">порыва́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to break with <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> someone</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порвать.html>порва́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всем</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уехать.html>уе́хал</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> далёкий <a href = vnd.unilang:город.html>го́род</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>porvál</b> so vsem i ujéxal v daljókij górod.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He <b>broke with</b> everything and left for a faraway town.</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">порыва́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:порезать.html>поре́завший</a> (13300)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порезать.html>поре́завший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">porézavšij</span>)

<ol><li>pornographic</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пора.html>по́р</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>гра<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:фи.html>фи́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>чес<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:кий.html>кий</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:относительный.html>относи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 3a✕~.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-порн-</b>; интерфикс: <b>-о-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-граф-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ическ</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ий</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порнография.html>порногра́фия</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pornográfija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порнография.html>порногра́фии</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порнография.html>порногра́фии</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:порнография.html>порногра́фий</a></b>)

<ol><li>pornography
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нравиться.html>нра́вится</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жестокий.html>жесто́кая</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порнография.html>порногра́фия</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jemú nrávitsja žestókaja <b>pornográfija</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He likes violent pornography.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́ла</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:думать.html>ду́мает</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порнография.html>порногра́фия</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:унижать.html>унижа́ет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:женщина.html>же́нщин</a>. «<a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голубой.html>голуба́я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порнография.html>порногра́фия</a></b>?» — <a href = vnd.unilang:спросить.html>спроси́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>Как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:следовать.html>сле́довало</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ожидать.html>ожида́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:промолчать.html>промолча́ла</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oná skazála, što dúmajet, što <b>pornográfija</b> unižájet žénščin. “A kak že golubája <b>pornográfija</b>?” — sprosíl ja. Kak i slédovalo ožidátʹ, oná promolčála.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">She said that she thinks pornography degrades women. "What about gay porn?" I asked. Unsurprisingly, she remained silent.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
